\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l02258}02258\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ For\ floating\ point\ numbers\ the\ numerical\ precision\ of\ sum\ (and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l02259}02259\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}np.add.reduce\`{}\`{})\ is\ in\ general\ limited\ by\ directly\ adding\ each\ number}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l02260}02260\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ individually\ to\ the\ result\ causing\ rounding\ errors\ in\ every\ step.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l02261}02261\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ However,\ often\ numpy\ will\ use\ a\ \ numerically\ better\ approach\ (partial}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l02262}02262\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ pairwise\ summation)\ leading\ to\ improved\ precision\ in\ many\ use-\/cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l02263}02263\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ This\ improved\ precision\ is\ always\ provided\ when\ no\ \`{}\`{}axis\`{}\`{}\ is\ given.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l02264}02264\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ When\ \`{}\`{}axis\`{}\`{}\ is\ given,\ it\ will\ depend\ on\ which\ axis\ is\ summed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l02265}02265\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Technically,\ to\ provide\ the\ best\ speed\ possible,\ the\ improved\ precision}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l02266}02266\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ is\ only\ used\ when\ the\ summation\ is\ along\ the\ fast\ axis\ in\ memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l02267}02267\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Note\ that\ the\ exact\ precision\ may\ vary\ depending\ on\ other\ parameters.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l02268}02268\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ In\ contrast\ to\ NumPy,\ Python's\ \`{}\`{}math.fsum\`{}\`{}\ function\ uses\ a\ slower\ but}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l02269}02269\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ more\ precise\ approach\ to\ summation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l02270}02270\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Especially\ when\ summing\ a\ large\ number\ of\ lower\ precision\ floating\ point}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03578}03578\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ deviations\ from\ the\ mean,\ i.e.,\ \`{}\`{}std\ =\ sqrt(mean(x))\`{}\`{},\ where}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03579}03579\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}x\ =\ abs(a\ -\/\ a.mean())**2\`{}\`{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03580}03580\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03581}03581\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ The\ average\ squared\ deviation\ is\ typically\ calculated\ as\ \`{}\`{}x.sum()\ /\ N\`{}\`{},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03582}03582\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ where\ \`{}\`{}N\ =\ len(x)\`{}\`{}.\ If,\ however,\ \`{}ddof\`{}\ is\ specified,\ the\ divisor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03583}03583\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}N\ -\/\ ddof\`{}\`{}\ is\ used\ instead.\ In\ standard\ statistical\ practice,\ \`{}\`{}ddof=1\`{}\`{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03584}03584\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ provides\ an\ unbiased\ estimator\ of\ the\ variance\ of\ the\ infinite\ population.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03585}03585\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}ddof=0\`{}\`{}\ provides\ a\ maximum\ likelihood\ estimate\ of\ the\ variance\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03586}03586\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ normally\ distributed\ variables.\ The\ standard\ deviation\ computed\ in\ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03587}03587\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ function\ is\ the\ square\ root\ of\ the\ estimated\ variance,\ so\ even\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03588}03588\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}ddof=1\`{}\`{},\ it\ will\ not\ be\ an\ unbiased\ estimate\ of\ the\ standard\ deviation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03589}03589\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ per\ se.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03590}03590\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03591}03591\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Note\ that,\ for\ complex\ numbers,\ \`{}std\`{}\ takes\ the\ absolute}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03592}03592\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ value\ before\ squaring,\ so\ that\ the\ result\ is\ always\ real\ and\ nonnegative.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03593}03593\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03594}03594\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ For\ floating-\/point\ input,\ the\ *std*\ is\ computed\ using\ the\ same}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03595}03595\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ precision\ the\ input\ has.\ Depending\ on\ the\ input\ data,\ this\ can\ cause}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03596}03596\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ the\ results\ to\ be\ inaccurate,\ especially\ for\ float32\ (see\ example\ below).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03597}03597\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Specifying\ a\ higher-\/accuracy\ accumulator\ using\ the\ \`{}dtype\`{}\ keyword\ can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03598}03598\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ alleviate\ this\ issue.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{core_2fromnumeric_8py_source_l03720}03720\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ i.e.,\ \ \`{}\`{}var\ =\ mean(x)\`{}\`{},\ where\ \`{}\`{}x\ =\ abs(a\ -\/\ a.mean())**2\`{}\`{}.}}
